rode alighted amadis caused squire vnarme damosel saw faire honest conuersation well pleased companie supped together merily afterward gaue pallad rest vpon neuerthelesse parted demaunded whether trauailed court king lisuart answered amadis replied damosel sée shall happen lady one best noble countrey hath committed welfare triall combate must within dayes following perfourmed king lisuart yet know man whome cause must defended one best knight great brittayne said amadis knight much estéemed especially among many good dardan answered damsel whome lately came cause said amadis ariseth combat pray ye faire lady know let vnderstand sir quoth one dardan loueth knight daughter countrey second nuptials maryed speake hath damosell beloued dardan conceiued hatred faire mother hath said friend neuer loue except bring king lisuarts court openly maintayne poore ladyes good appertaineth one gainesay iustifie combat news highly pleasing amadis meanes intended compasse occasion reuenged wrong presence oriana perceiue knight made enter thought damosel well noting one thus spake pray ye sir courtesie acquaint v reason sudden musing may without offence knowne faire lady answered amadis promise loyall gentlewoman kéepe secret reueale one willingly shall tell ye sollemnely sware perfourme intend quoth combate dame spake mind faile would haue concealed selues heard said much abashed notwithstanding made great estéeme séeing vttered praise dardan could affray would hazard combat therefore alreadie broken matter thus replyed gentle sir intent procéedeth high resolued minde pray prosperous successe gaue eche good night went rest till morning dislodged together intreated damosel seeing went place forrest kept men euill hauiour therefore would forsake companie whereof made promise along ride sundry discoursings among talke desired respect met happily together would content let knowe name name quoth amadis pray ye kéepe selues procéeding vaste vnfrequented place one day
